href="#cite_note-148">&#91;148&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Laverbread" class="mw-redirect" title="Laverbread">Laverbread</a> is made using a puree of seaweed, and is traditionally served with a Welsh breakfast.<sup id="cite_ref-149" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-149">&#91;149&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Welsh_cakes" class="mw-redirect" title="Welsh cakes">Welsh cakes</a> are made on a <a href="/wiki/Bakestone" title="Bakestone">bakestone</a>, and are small round spiced cakes containing <a href="/wiki/Raisins" class="mw-redirect" title="Raisins">raisins</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sultana_(dried_grape)" class="mw-redirect" title="Sultana (dried grape)">sultanas</a> and occasionally <a href="/wiki/Currant_(grape)" class="mw-redirect" title="Currant (grape)">currants</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-150" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-150">&#91;150&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Bara_brith" title="Bara brith">Bara brith</a> contains similar ingredients to Welsh cakes, but is similar to a <a href="/wiki/Tea_bread" class="mw-redirect" title="Tea bread">tea bread</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-151" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-151">&#91;151&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Crempog_-_Anglesey_style.JPG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/Crempog_-_Anglesey_style.JPG/220px-Crempog_-_Anglesey_style.JPG" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/Crempog_-_Anglesey_style.JPG/330px-Crempog_-_Anglesey_style.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/Crempog_-_Anglesey_style.JPG/440px-Crempog_-_Anglesey_style.JPG 2x" data-file-width="5184" data-file-height="3888" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Crempog_-_Anglesey_style.JPG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Crempog - Anglesey style</div></div></div>
<p>The Welsh have their own versions of <a href="/wiki/Pancakes" class="mw-redirect" title="Pancakes">pancakes</a>, <a href="/wiki/Crempog" title="Crempog">Crempog</a>'s (sometimes called ffroes) are considerably thick. They are traditionally layered on top of each other to form a large cake. Some are very much like American pancakes, others may be made with yeast (called crempog furum) or oatmeal (although this is also true of American pancakes) and some are like Scotch pancakes.<sup id="cite_ref-152" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-152">&#91;152&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-153" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-153">&#91;153&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Beer" title="Beer">Beer</a> is the <a href="/wiki/Beer_in_Wales" title="Beer in Wales">national drink</a> of Wales, despite the influence of the <a href="/wiki/Temperance_movement" title="Temperance movement">temperance movement</a> in Wales.<sup id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEDavies200857_154-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEDavies200857-154">&#91;154&#93;</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Wrexham_Lager" class="mw-redirect" title="Wrexham Lager">Wrexham Lager Beer Company</a> was the first successful <a href="/wiki/Lager" title="Lager">lager</a> producer in Britain when it opened in 1882<sup id="cite_ref-155" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-155">&#91;155&#93;</a></sup> and the <a href="/wiki/Felinfoel_Brewery" title="Felinfoel Brewery">Felinfoel Brewery</a> was the first brewery in Europe to put beer in cans.<sup id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEDavies200857_154-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEDavies200857-154">&#91;154&#93;</a></sup> Whisky production in Wales was historically a niche industry, and completely shut down in 1910 when the last distillery was bought out by a Scottish firm. However, the <a href="/wiki/Penderyn_(whisky)" title="Penderyn (whisky)">Penderyn</a> distillery became the first Wales-created whisky in a century to go on sale when it was launched in 2004.<sup id="cite_ref-156" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-156">&#91;156&#93;</a></sup> There are 20 Welsh <a href="/wiki/Vineyards" class="mw-redirect" title="Vineyards">vineyards</a> producing 100,000 bottles of wine a year in total.<sup id="cite_ref-157" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-157">&#91;157&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEFreeman199619_158-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEFreeman199619-158">&#91;158&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="See_also">See also</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Culture_of_Wales&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: See also">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div role="navigation" aria-label="Portals" class="noprint portal plainlist tright" style="margin:0.5em 0 0.5em 1em;border:solid #aaa 1px">

<li style="display:table-row"><span style="display:table-cell;padding:0.2em;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center"><img alt="flag" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Flag_of_Wales_%281959%E2%80%93present%29.svg/32px-Flag_of_Wales_%281959%E2%80%93present%29.svg.png" width="32" height="19" class="noviewer thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Flag_of_Wales_%281959%E2%80%93present%29.svg/48px-Flag_of_Wales_%281959%E2%80%93present%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Flag_of_Wales_%281959%E2%80%93present%29.svg/64px-Flag_of_Wales_%281959%E2%80%93present%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="830" data-file-height="498" /></span><span style="display:table-cell;padding:0.2em 0.2em 0.2em 0.3em;vertical-align:middle"><a href="/wiki/Portal:Wales" title="Portal:Wales">Wales portal</a></span></li></ul></div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Notes">Notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Culture_of_Wales&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="reflist columns references-column-width" style="-moz-column-width: 30em; -webkit-column-width: 30em; column-width: 30em; list-style-type: decimal;">
<ol class="references">
<li id="cite_note-FOOTNOTEDavies19933-1"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-FOOTNOTEDavies19933_1-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="#CITEREFDavies1993">Davies 1993</a>, p.&#160;3.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-FOOTNOTEJonesMattingly1990153-2"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-FOOTNOTEJonesMattingly1990153_2-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="#CITEREFJonesMattingly1990">Jones &amp; Mattingly 1990</a>, p.&#160;153.</span>
</li>
